Doubts Still Exist About the Reduction of American Cotton Fields

A telegram from New York on the 27th reports on the cotton market for the week: The Agricultural Administration has abandoned maintaining new wheat. Although its future policy on cotton has not been determined, the hearts of people in the exchange are uneasy. The old bulls are carrying out large-scale settlements. However, their supply during the price decline is absorbed by domestic and foreign peers. The South sells very little. The real position has improved due to the settlement of bulls. However, speculators are limited in purchasing because the statistics are favorable to shorts and there are still doubts about the reduction of cotton fields. There are also several places where cotton field work has been delayed due to rain, but the soil has benefited. According to official sources, the policy of the Agricultural Administration will not be expressed until the new cotton has considerable certainty. The Flour Market Is Weak and Depressed

Yesterday, the flour market generally showed a state of hovering. At the beginning of this month, it was still flat, followed by one fall after another. Actual sales were still smooth in terms of temporary buying for sales purposes, so the market atmosphere was slightly firmer. Although the remote Ming Dynasty months once showed a firm and brisk image in the morning, most bulls, in view of the current good flour sales, were still unable to maintain it. Later, as soon as the spot goods accumulated, they were deeply afraid of the increased squeeze in the future, so they gradually returned, which led to the market atmosphere becoming weak and depressed again. As a result, this month was up by 5 li compared to the previous day, April and May were down by a small 2 li and a half, June was down by a small 5 li, and July and August were unchanged.

Futures Wheat Near Up, Far Down

Yesterday, the futures wheat market generally showed a state of ups and downs. The overseas wheat quotation was slightly better, and the hearts of people outside the industry were slightly better. The market atmosphere for the next month was slightly better because the end of March was good, and in view of the identity relationship of overseas wheat, the market atmosphere was associated with April, so the market atmosphere was slightly better in the midst of hovering. The distant period was still in a bad environment, and Citibank wheat was still available for sale between 4 taels, and the official was reluctant to sell for a small number of dollars, and refused to sell unless it was a huge amount. In this situation, the future is really hard to say. As a result, April and May were up by 2 fen compared to the previous day, June was unchanged, July was down by a small 2 fen, and August was down by a small 1 fen.

North and South Goods: Longan Meat Market Trend Weak

Longan meat has been slow to sell lately because there is not much stock and because various gangs are also selling it very slowly. As a result, the market trend has gradually become weak. The opening price of top and middle grade goods has not been above 40 taels recently, and the opening price of ordinary goods is 30 taels. Each store is unwilling to continue to loosen the top dried longan meat, because they are short of stock, which has decreased by 1-2 taels compared to the previous one. The lower grade goods are not above 28 taels, but the market plate is quite accommodating because the market is not smooth. It is difficult to turn around for the time being.

Silk and Tea: Morocco Has a Large Stock of Tea

Morocco is the largest market for green tea in our country. In recent years, Zhenmei, Pearl Tea, Needle Eyebrow, and Xiumei have been shipped to the area by British and French merchants. Therefore, the prosperity or stagnation of the tea market there is closely related to the sales of green tea in our country. It is now known that although the green tea market in Morocco is slightly more active than last year, the tea price is quite low and tea merchants are not profitable. At present, there are still 75,000 boxes of various kinds of Zhenmei Pearl Tea in stock, and no less than 100,000 boxes including those not yet shipped from Shanghai. This year's new tea will be launched in a blink of an eye, but the sales overseas are not prosperous, and the stock is abundant. The future is difficult to be optimistic.
